It may\n  //    use inline healthcheck (i.e. consider endpoint UNHEALTHY if connection\n  //    failed to a particular endpoint to account for health status propagation\n  //    delay between HDS and EDS).\n  // By default, can_healthcheck is true. The envoyproxy/data-plane-api repository contains 40 .proto files that define xDS (Extensible Discovery Service) service declarations for control plane communication. These services include discovery services (AggregatedDiscoveryService, ClusterDiscoveryService, EndpointDiscoveryService, ListenerDiscoveryService, RouteDiscoveryService, SecretDiscoveryService), load reporting services (LoadReportingService), health checking (HealthDiscoveryService), and various gRPC service definitions (AccessLogService, Authorization, RateLimitService, MetricsService, ExternalProcessor, etc.). The grpc/grpc repository implements the standard gRPC Health service (grpc_health_v1.Health) across multiple languages. The Health proto definition is located at src/proto/grpc/health/v1/health.proto and src/python/grpcio_health_checking/grpc_health/v1/health.proto, with implementations provided in C++ (src/cpp/server/health/), Python (src/python/grpcio_health_checking/grpc_health/v1/health.py), and Ruby (src/ruby/pb/grpc/health/v1/health_services_pb.rb). The Health service defines two RPCs: Check and Watch for liveness/readiness probing. The gRPC repository uses the xDS services from data-plane-api for its control plane implementation, particularly the AggregatedDiscoveryService and LoadReportingService, as evidenced by references in xds_transport_fake.h and xds_server.h test infrastructure.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":335,"cache_read_input_tokens":50590,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":335},"output_tokens":5,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"66f183e2-3464-47a6-bcac-f54ef6b4f7bb","uuid":"252f4f02-7d5a-48e4-8342-45b98e5e47ad"}
